+func contractToProduct(contract *models.Contract, h *models.Handset) *handset.ContractProduct {
+    name := contract.HandsetName
+    basePrice := parsePenceOrZero(contract.RetailPrice)
+    monthlyRepayment := parsePenceOrZero(contract.ContractPrice)
+
+    if h != nil {
+        if name == "" {
+            name = h.CurrentProperties.Name
+        }
+        if basePrice == 0 {
+            basePrice = h.CurrentProperties.RRPPence
+        }
+        if monthlyRepayment == 0 {
+            monthlyRepayment = h.CurrentProperties.RentalPricePence
+        }
+    }
+
+    // Avoid int->int32 wraparound on unexpected/corrupted data.
+    basePrice32 := int32(0)
+    if basePrice >= math.MinInt32 && basePrice <= math.MaxInt32 {
+        basePrice32 = int32(basePrice) // nolint: gosec
+    }
+    monthlyRepayment32 := int32(0)
+    if monthlyRepayment >= math.MinInt32 && monthlyRepayment <= math.MaxInt32 {
+        monthlyRepayment32 = int32(monthlyRepayment) // nolint: gosec
+    }
+
+    return &handset.ContractProduct{
+        Id:               contract.HandsetID,
+        Name:             name,
+        BasePrice:        basePrice32,
+        MonthlyRepayment: monthlyRepayment32,
+    }
+}
+
+func parsePenceOrZero(s string) int {
+    if s == "" {
+        return 0
+    }
+    v, err := strconv.Atoi(s)
+    if err != nil {
+        return 0
+    }
+    return v
+}
+

     if err != nil {

@@ -260,44 +363,55 @@ func recordRequestMetric(method string, err error) {

+    if err := s.store.UpdateContractEligibilityFailed(ctx, requestID, outcome); err != nil {
+        return fmt.Errorf("failed to update contract status: %w", err)
+    }
+
+    if err := s.eventProducer.ProduceMobileHandsetContractDeclinedSync(ctx, &serviceevents.MobileHandsetContractDeclined{
+        ServiceId:  contract.ServiceID,
+        CustomerId: contract.CustomerID,
+        ContractId: contract.ID.String(),
+        HandsetId:  contract.HandsetID,
+    }); err != nil {
+        tlog.WithError(err).
+            WithAttribute("contract_id", contract.ID.String()).
+            Error(ctx, "failed to produce MobileHandsetContractDeclined event")
+    }
+
+    tlog.WithAttribute("request_id", requestID).
+        WithAttribute("contract_id", contract.ID.String()).
+        Info(ctx, "eligibility failed, contract declined")
+
+    return nil
 }
 
-func mergeHandsetDetails(contractHandset, catalogueHandset handsetdb.Handset) handsetdb.Handset {

+// EligibilityStatusUpdate handles status update notifications from the eligibility provider.
+// For DECLINED and WITHDRAWN statuses, the contract is moved to DECLINED.
+func (s *Service) EligibilityStatusUpdate(ctx context.Context, requestID, statusStr string) error {
+    // @todo matt - this is a bit of a catch-all for any future status updates from the eligibility provider that require action. we don't really know what the statuses in the proto actually represent at this stage, neither do we know which are terminal states and how they should interact with the success/failure callbacks. consider this method WIP for the time being.
+    if requestID == "" {
+        return fmt.Errorf("request_id is required: %w", terrors.ErrBadRequest)
     }
-    if contractHandset.ContractPrice == "" {
-        contractHandset.ContractPrice = catalogueHandset.ContractPrice
+
+    if statusStr != "DECLINED" && statusStr != "WITHDRAWN" {
+        tlog.WithAttribute("request_id", requestID).
+            WithAttribute("status", statusStr).
+            Info(ctx, "eligibility status update received, no action required")
+        return nil
     }
-    if contractHandset.RetailPrice == "" {
-        contractHandset.RetailPrice = catalogueHandset.RetailPrice
+
+    contract, err := s.store.GetContractByRequestID(ctx, requestID)
+    if err != nil {
+        return fmt.Errorf("failed to get contract: %w", err)
     }
-    if contractHandset.ContractTerm == "" {
-        contractHandset.ContractTerm = catalogueHandset.ContractTerm
+
+    if contract.Status != models.ContractStatusPendingEligibility {
+        tlog.WithAttribute("request_id", requestID).
+            WithAttribute("current_status", string(contract.Status)).
+            Info(ctx, "eligibility status update ignored, contract is not pending eligibility")
+        return nil
+    }
+
+    if err := s.store.UpdateContractStatus(ctx, requestID, models.ContractStatusDeclined); err != nil {
+        return fmt.Errorf("failed to update contract status: %w", err)
+    }
+
+    if err := s.eventProducer.ProduceMobileHandsetContractDeclinedSync(ctx, &serviceevents.MobileHandsetContractDeclined{
+        ServiceId:  contract.ServiceID,
+        CustomerId: contract.CustomerID,
+        ContractId: contract.ID.String(),
+        HandsetId:  contract.HandsetID,
+    }); err != nil {
+        tlog.WithError(err).
+            WithAttribute("contract_id", contract.ID.String()).
+            Error(ctx, "failed to produce MobileHandsetContractDeclined event")
+    }
+
+    tlog.WithAttribute("request_id", requestID).
+        WithAttribute("contract_id", contract.ID.String()).
+        WithAttribute("status", statusStr).
+        Info(ctx, "eligibility status update, contract declined")
+
+    return nil
+}
+
+// money converts a pence integer string (e.g. "4200") to a Money message with
+// the amount expressed in pounds (e.g. "42.00"). The Money type is consumed by
+// downstream services that treat Amount as a decimal pound value.
+func money(penceStr string) *serviceevents.Money {
+    pence, err := strconv.Atoi(penceStr)
+    if err != nil {
+        return &serviceevents.Money{Amount: penceStr, Currency: currencyGBP}
+    }
+    return &serviceevents.Money{
+        Amount:   fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", float64(pence)/100),
+        Currency: currencyGBP,
     }
-    return contractHandset
 }

+func (m *MockDoer) Do(opts ...googleapi.CallOption) (*sheets.ValueRange, error) {
+    m.ctrl.T.Helper()
+    varargs := []any{}
+    for _, a := range opts {
+        varargs = append(varargs, a)
+    }
+    ret := m.ctrl.Call(m, "Do", varargs...)
+    ret0, _ := ret[0].(*sheets.ValueRange)
+    ret1, _ := ret[1].(error)
+    return ret0, ret1
+}
+
+// Do indicates an expected call of Do.
+func (mr *MockDoerMockRecorder) Do(opts ...any) *gomock.Call {
+    mr.mock.ctrl.T.Helper()
+    return mr.mock.ctrl.RecordCallWithMethodType(mr.mock, "Do", reflect.TypeOf((*MockDoer)(nil).Do), opts...)
+}
+
+// MockHandsetUpserter is a mock of HandsetUpserter interface.
+type MockHandsetUpserter struct {
+    ctrl     *gomock.Controller
+    recorder *MockHandsetUpserterMockRecorder
+    isgomock struct{}
+}

+// MockHandsetUpserterMockRecorder is the mock recorder for MockHandsetUpserter.

+}

+    return mock
+}

+}

+package sheet

+    valueTrue  = "TRUE"
+    valueFalse = "FALSE"

+// validRow returns a 22-element row with all fields filled in correctly.
+func validRow() []interface{} {
+    row := make([]interface{}, colCount)
+    row[colName] = "iPhone 15"
+    row[colColours] = "Black, White"
+    row[colRentalPricePence] = "42.00"
+    row[colRRPPence] = "999.00"
+    row[colContractTermMonths] = "24"
+    row[colManufacturer] = "Apple"
+    row[colModel] = "A3090"
+    row[colCapacity] = "128GB"
+    row[colScreenSize] = "6.1\""
+    row[colBattery] = "3227 mAh"
+    row[colSDCapacity] = ""
+    row[colWiFiStandard] = "Wi-Fi 6"
+    row[colESim] = valueTrue
+    row[colDualSim] = valueFalse
+    row[colSaleStatus] = "Active"
+    row[colIsNew] = valueTrue
+    row[colUWLaunchDate] = "2024-01-15"
+    row[colPriceChange] = valueFalse
+    row[colEndOfLife] = valueFalse
+    row[colSpecificationsLink] = "https://spec.example.com"
+    row[colShouldHide] = valueFalse
+    row[colBillID] = "BILL-123"
+    return row
+}

+func TestParseHandsetRow_Valid(t *testing.T) {
+    row := validRow()
+    h, err := parseHandsetRow(row)
+    if err != nil {
+        t.Fatalf("unexpected error: %v", err)
+    }
+
+    p := h.CurrentProperties
+    if h.BillID != "BILL-123" {
+        t.Errorf("BillID: got %q, want %q", h.BillID, "BILL-123")
+    }
+    if p.Name != "iPhone 15" {
+        t.Errorf("Name: got %q, want %q", p.Name, "iPhone 15")
+    }
+    if p.RentalPricePence != 4200 {
+        t.Errorf("RentalPricePence: got %d, want 4200", p.RentalPricePence)
+    }
+    if p.RRPPence != 99900 {
+        t.Errorf("RRPPence: got %d, want 99900", p.RRPPence)
+    }
+    if p.ContractTermMonths != 24 {
+        t.Errorf("ContractTermMonths: got %d, want 24", p.ContractTermMonths)
+    }
+    if !p.ESim {
+        t.Error("ESim: got false, want true")
+    }
+    if p.DualSim {
+        t.Error("DualSim: got true, want false")
+    }
+    if !p.IsNew {
+        t.Error("IsNew: got false, want true")
+    }
+    expectedDate := time.Date(2024, 1, 15, 0, 0, 0, 0, time.UTC)
+    if !p.UWLaunchDate.Equal(expectedDate) {
+        t.Errorf("UWLaunchDate: got %v, want %v", p.UWLaunchDate, expectedDate)
+    }
+    if p.Version == "" {
+        t.Error("Version must not be empty")
+    }
+}
+
+func TestParseHandsetRow_VersionDeterminism(t *testing.T) {
+    h1, err := parseHandsetRow(validRow())
+    if err != nil {
+        t.Fatal(err)
+    }
+    h2, err := parseHandsetRow(validRow())
+    if err != nil {
+        t.Fatal(err)
+    }
+    if h1.CurrentProperties.Version != h2.CurrentProperties.Version {
+        t.Errorf("version not deterministic: %q vs %q",
+            h1.CurrentProperties.Version, h2.CurrentProperties.Version)
+    }
+}
+
+func TestParseHandsetRow_VersionChangesWithContent(t *testing.T) {
+    row := validRow()
+    h1, _ := parseHandsetRow(row)
+
+    row[colRentalPricePence] = "50.00"
+    h2, _ := parseHandsetRow(row)
+
+    if h1.CurrentProperties.Version == h2.CurrentProperties.Version {
+        t.Error("version should differ when rental price changes")
+    }
+}
+

+func TestParseHandsetRow_BoolVariants(t *testing.T) {
+    truthy := []string{"TRUE", "true", "Yes", "yes", "1"}
+    falsy := []string{"FALSE", "false", "No", "no", "0", ""}
+
+    for _, v := range truthy {
+        row := validRow()
+        row[colESim] = v
+        h, err := parseHandsetRow(row)
+        if err != nil {
+            t.Errorf("value %q: unexpected error: %v", v, err)
+            continue
+        }
+        if !h.CurrentProperties.ESim {
+            t.Errorf("value %q: expected ESim true", v)
+        }
+    }
+
+    for _, v := range falsy {
+        row := validRow()
+        row[colESim] = v
+        h, err := parseHandsetRow(row)
+        if err != nil {
+            t.Errorf("value %q: unexpected error: %v", v, err)
+            continue
+        }
+        if h.CurrentProperties.ESim {
+            t.Errorf("value %q: expected ESim false", v)
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+func TestParseHandsetRow_PricesConvertedToPence(t *testing.T) {
+    cases := []struct {
+        pounds        string
+        expectedPence int
+    }{
+        {"0.01", 1},
+        {"1.00", 100},
+        {"25.50", 2550},
+        {"999.99", 99999},
+    }
+
+    for _, tc := range cases {
+        row := validRow()
+        row[colRentalPricePence] = tc.pounds
+        row[colRRPPence] = tc.pounds
+        h, err := parseHandsetRow(row)
+        if err != nil {
+            t.Errorf("pounds %q: unexpected error: %v", tc.pounds, err)
+            continue
+        }
+        if h.CurrentProperties.RentalPricePence != tc.expectedPence {
+            t.Errorf("pounds %q: RentalPricePence got %d, want %d",
+                tc.pounds, h.CurrentProperties.RentalPricePence, tc.expectedPence)
+        }
+        if h.CurrentProperties.RRPPence != tc.expectedPence {
+            t.Errorf("pounds %q: RRPPence got %d, want %d",
+                tc.pounds, h.CurrentProperties.RRPPence, tc.expectedPence)
+        }
+    }
+}

+++ b/services/handset/internal/sheet/sheet.go

+package sheet
+
+import (
+    "context"
+    "fmt"
+    "strconv"
+    "time"
+
+    "github.com/google/uuid"
+    "google.golang.org/api/googleapi"
+    "google.golang.org/api/sheets/v4"
+
+    "github.com/utilitywarehouse/telecom-mobile/pkg/libdry/tlog"
+    "github.com/utilitywarehouse/telecom-mobile/services/handset/internal/models"
+)
+
+// Column indices within each sheet row (A=0 … V=21).
+// A: Handset Name, B: Colours, C: Current Rental Price, D: RRP,
+// E: Contract Term, F: Manufacturer, G: Model, H: Capacity,
+// I: Screen Size, J: Battery, K: SD Card Slot, L: Wi-Fi Standard,
+// M: E-Sim, N: Dual Sim, O: Status, P: New, Q: UW Launch Date,
+// R: Price Change, S: End of Life, T: Specifications Link, U: Hide, V: Bill ID
+const (
+    colName               = 0
+    colColours            = 1
+    colRentalPricePence   = 2
+    colRRPPence           = 3
+    colContractTermMonths = 4
+    colManufacturer       = 5
+    colModel              = 6
+    colCapacity           = 7
+    colScreenSize         = 8
+    colBattery            = 9
+    colSDCapacity         = 10
+    colWiFiStandard       = 11
+    colESim               = 12
+    colDualSim            = 13
+    colSaleStatus         = 14
+    colIsNew              = 15
+    colUWLaunchDate       = 16
+    colPriceChange        = 17
+    colEndOfLife          = 18
+    colSpecificationsLink = 19
+    colShouldHide         = 20
+    colBillID             = 21
+    colCount              = 22
+)
+
+const uwLaunchDateLayout = "2006-01-02"
+
+//go:generate mockgen -destination=./mocks/$GOFILE -source=./$GOFILE -package=mocks
+type SheetValueGetter interface {
+    Get(sheetID, readRange string) Doer
+}
+
+type Doer interface {
+    Do(opts ...googleapi.CallOption) (*sheets.ValueRange, error)
+}
+
+type ValueGetter struct {
+    Svc *sheets.Service
+}
+
+type HandsetUpserter interface {
+    UpsertHandsetModel(ctx context.Context, handset models.Handset) error
+}
+
+func (s *ValueGetter) Get(sheetID, readRange string) Doer {
+    return s.Svc.Spreadsheets.Values.Get(sheetID, readRange)
+}
+
+type Service struct {
+    sheetID           string
+    readRange         string
+    sheetValuesGetter SheetValueGetter
+    store             HandsetUpserter
+}
+
+func NewSheetService(sheetID, readRange string, sheetValuesGetter SheetValueGetter, store HandsetUpserter) (*Service, error) {
+    return &Service{
+        sheetID:           sheetID,
+        readRange:         readRange,
+        sheetValuesGetter: sheetValuesGetter,
+        store:             store,
+    }, nil
+}
+
+func (s *Service) UpdateHandsets(ctx context.Context) {
+    handsets, err := s.getHandsetsFromSheet(ctx)
+    if err != nil {
+        tlog.WithError(err).Error(ctx, "failed to fetch handsets from sheet")
+        return
+    }
+
+    for _, handset := range handsets {
+        if err := s.store.UpsertHandsetModel(ctx, handset); err != nil {
+            tlog.WithError(err).Error(ctx, "failed to upsert handset")
+            // @todo should we alert
+            return
+        }
+    }
+    return
+}
+
+func (s *Service) getHandsetsFromSheet(ctx context.Context) ([]models.Handset, error) {
+    tlog.Debug(ctx, "fetching whitelist via sheets API")
+
+    // Load your service account key JSON file
+    resp, err := s.sheetValuesGetter.Get(s.sheetID, s.readRange).Do()
+    if err != nil {
+        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to retrieve handsets from sheet: %w", err)
+    }
+
+    if len(resp.Values) == 0 {
+        tlog.Warn(ctx, "no handsets found")
+        return nil, nil
+    }
+    tlog.Debug(ctx, "sheet values: %+v", resp.Values)
+
+    var handsets []models.Handset
+    for _, row := range resp.Values {
+        tlog.Debug(ctx, "row: %+v", row)
+        if len(row) < 2 {
+            continue // skip rows that don’t have at least two columns
+        }
+
+        handset, err := parseHandsetRow(row)
+        if err != nil {
+            tlog.WithError(err).Warn(ctx, "failed to parse handset row, skipping")
+            continue
+        }
+        handsets = append(handsets, handset)
+    }
+
+    if len(handsets) == 0 {
+        tlog.Warn(ctx, "no valid handsets found in sheet")
+        return nil, nil
+    }
+
+    return handsets, nil
+}
+
+func parseHandsetRow(row []interface{}) (models.Handset, error) {
+    if len(row) < colCount {
+        return models.Handset{}, fmt.Errorf("row has %d columns, expected at least %d", len(row), colCount)
+    }
+
+    col := func(i int) string {
+        if v, ok := row[i].(string); ok {
+            return v
+        }
+        return fmt.Sprintf("%v", row[i])
+    }
+
+    // Prices in the sheet are pounds (e.g. "25.00"); store as pence.
+    parsePencef := func(i int) (int, error) {
+        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(col(i), 64)
+        if err != nil {
+            return 0, fmt.Errorf("column %d: invalid price %q: %w", i, col(i), err)
+        }
+        // Round to avoid float truncation errors (e.g. "999.99" -> 99998.999...).
+        return int(f*100 + 0.5), nil
+    }
+
+    parseBool := func(i int) (bool, error) {
+        switch col(i) {
+        case "TRUE", "true", "Yes", "yes", "1":
+            return true, nil
+        case "FALSE", "false", "No", "no", "0", "":
+            return false, nil
+        default:
+            return false, fmt.Errorf("column %d: invalid bool %q", i, col(i))
+        }
+    }
+
+    rentalPricePence, err := parsePencef(colRentalPricePence)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    rrpPence, err := parsePencef(colRRPPence)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    contractTermMonths, err := strconv.Atoi(col(colContractTermMonths))
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, fmt.Errorf("column %d: invalid contractTermMonths %q: %w", colContractTermMonths, col(colContractTermMonths), err)
+    }
+
+    eSim, err := parseBool(colESim)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    dualSim, err := parseBool(colDualSim)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    isNew, err := parseBool(colIsNew)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    priceChange, err := parseBool(colPriceChange)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    endOfLife, err := parseBool(colEndOfLife)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    shouldHide, err := parseBool(colShouldHide)
+    if err != nil {
+        return models.Handset{}, err
+    }
+
+    var uwLaunchDate time.Time
+    if d := col(colUWLaunchDate); d != "" {
+        uwLaunchDate, err = time.Parse(uwLaunchDateLayout, d)
+        if err != nil {
+            return models.Handset{}, fmt.Errorf("column %d: invalid uwLaunchDate %q: %w", colUWLaunchDate, d, err)
+        }
+    }
+
+    billID := col(colBillID)
+    if billID == "" {
+        return models.Handset{}, fmt.Errorf("billID (column %d) is required", colBillID)
+    }
+
+    props := models.HandsetProperties{
+        Name:               col(colName),
+        Colours:            col(colColours),
+        RentalPricePence:   rentalPricePence,
+        RRPPence:           rrpPence,
+        ContractTermMonths: contractTermMonths,
+        Manufacturer:       col(colManufacturer),
+        Model:              col(colModel),
+        Capacity:           col(colCapacity),
+        ScreenSize:         col(colScreenSize),
+        Battery:            col(colBattery),
+        SDCapacity:         col(colSDCapacity),
+        WiFiStandard:       col(colWiFiStandard),
+        ESim:               eSim,
+        DualSim:            dualSim,
+        SaleStatus:         col(colSaleStatus),
+        IsNew:              isNew,
+        UWLaunchDate:       uwLaunchDate,
+        PriceChange:        priceChange,
+        EndOfLife:          endOfLife,
+        SpecificationsLink: col(colSpecificationsLink),
+        BillID:             billID,
+    }
+
+    // Derive a deterministic version from all mutable properties so the
+    // storage layer can detect when something has changed and archive the old values.
+    versionSeed := fmt.Sprintf("%s|%s|%d|%d|%d|%s|%s|%s|%s|%s|%s|%s|%s|%t|%t|%s|%t|%s|%t|%t|%s",
+        billID, props.Name,
+        rentalPricePence, rrpPence, contractTermMonths,
+        props.Manufacturer, props.Model, props.Colours, props.Capacity,
+        props.ScreenSize, props.Battery, props.SDCapacity, props.WiFiStandard,
+        eSim, dualSim, props.SaleStatus, isNew,
+        uwLaunchDate.Format(uwLaunchDateLayout), priceChange, endOfLife,
+        props.SpecificationsLink,
+    )
+    props.Version = uuid.NewSHA1(uuid.NameSpaceOID, []byte(versionSeed)).String()
+
+    // BillID is the stable identifier for this handset; stock is managed separately.
+    return models.Handset{
+        BillID:            billID,
+        CurrentProperties: props,
+        Active:            !shouldHide,
+    }, nil
+}

+package sheet_test
+
+import (
+    "context"
+    "errors"
+
+    . "github.com/onsi/ginkgo/v2"
+    . "github.com/onsi/gomega"
+    "go.uber.org/mock/gomock"
+    "google.golang.org/api/sheets/v4"
+
+    "github.com/utilitywarehouse/telecom-mobile/services/handset/internal/sheet"
+    "github.com/utilitywarehouse/telecom-mobile/services/handset/internal/sheet/mocks"
+)
+
+// fullRow returns a 22-element sheet row with valid values for all columns.
+func fullRow() []interface{} {
+    return []interface{}{
+        "iPhone 15",                // A: Name
+        "Black",                    // B: Colours
+        "42.00",                    // C: Rental price (£)
+        "999.00",                   // D: RRP (£)
+        "24",                       // E: Contract term months
+        "Apple",                    // F: Manufacturer
+        "A3090",                    // G: Model
+        "128GB",                    // H: Capacity
+        "6.1\"",                    // I: Screen size
+        "3227 mAh",                 // J: Battery
+        "",                         // K: SD capacity
+        "Wi-Fi 6",                  // L: Wi-Fi standard
+        "TRUE",                     // M: E-Sim
+        "FALSE",                    // N: Dual SIM
+        "Active",                   // O: Sale status
+        "TRUE",                     // P: Is new
+        "2024-01-15",               // Q: UW launch date
+        "FALSE",                    // R: Price change
+        "FALSE",                    // S: End of life
+        "https://spec.example.com", // T: Specifications link
+        "FALSE",                    // U: Should hide
+        "BILL-123",                 // V: Bill ID
+    }
+}
+
+var _ = Describe("Sheet Service", func() {
+    var (
+        ctrl       *gomock.Controller
+        mockGetter *mocks.MockSheetValueGetter
+        mockDoer   *mocks.MockDoer
+        mockStore  *mocks.MockHandsetUpserter
+        svc        *sheet.Service
+        ctx        context.Context
+    )
+
+    BeforeEach(func() {
+        ctrl = gomock.NewController(GinkgoT())
+        mockGetter = mocks.NewMockSheetValueGetter(ctrl)
+        mockDoer = mocks.NewMockDoer(ctrl)
+        mockStore = mocks.NewMockHandsetUpserter(ctrl)
+
+        var err error
+        svc, err = sheet.NewSheetService("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V", mockGetter, mockStore)
+        Expect(err).ToNot(HaveOccurred())
+
+        ctx = context.Background()
+    })
+
+    AfterEach(func() {
+        ctrl.Finish()
+    })
+
+    Describe("UpdateHandsets", func() {
+        When("the sheet API returns an error", func() {
+            It("logs and returns without calling the store", func() {
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(nil, errors.New("sheets API unavailable"))
+
+                // No store calls expected — the function should return early.
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+
+        When("the sheet returns no rows", func() {
+            It("does not call the store", func() {
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(&sheets.ValueRange{Values: nil}, nil)
+
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+
+        When("all rows are invalid", func() {
+            It("does not call the store", func() {
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(&sheets.ValueRange{
+                    Values: [][]interface{}{
+                        {"short"},       // too few columns
+                        {"only", "two"}, // still too few
+                    },
+                }, nil)
+
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+
+        When("the sheet returns valid rows", func() {
+            It("upserts each handset", func() {
+                row1 := fullRow()
+                row2 := fullRow()
+                row2[21] = "BILL-456" // different billID
+
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(&sheets.ValueRange{
+                    Values: [][]interface{}{row1, row2},
+                }, nil)
+
+                mockStore.EXPECT().
+                    UpsertHandsetModel(gomock.Any(), gomock.Any()).
+                    Return(nil).
+                    Times(2)
+
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+
+        When("a valid row is mixed with an invalid row", func() {
+            It("upserts the valid row and skips the invalid one", func() {
+                invalidRow := fullRow()
+                invalidRow[2] = "not-a-price" // bad rental price
+
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(&sheets.ValueRange{
+                    Values: [][]interface{}{invalidRow, fullRow()},
+                }, nil)
+
+                mockStore.EXPECT().
+                    UpsertHandsetModel(gomock.Any(), gomock.Any()).
+                    Return(nil).
+                    Times(1)
+
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+
+        When("the store returns an error on upsert", func() {
+            It("stops processing further rows", func() {
+                row1 := fullRow()
+                row2 := fullRow()
+                row2[21] = "BILL-456"
+
+                mockGetter.EXPECT().Get("sheet-id", "Sheet1!A:V").Return(mockDoer)
+                mockDoer.EXPECT().Do().Return(&sheets.ValueRange{
+                    Values: [][]interface{}{row1, row2},
+                }, nil)
+
+                // Only the first upsert is expected — the second is never reached.
+                mockStore.EXPECT().
+                    UpsertHandsetModel(gomock.Any(), gomock.Any()).
+                    Return(errors.New("mongo write error")).
+                    Times(1)
+
+                svc.UpdateHandsets(ctx)
+            })
+        })
+    })
+})

+// UpsertHandsetModel upserts a models.Handset with versioning support.
+// When currentProperties.Version changes, the old properties are pushed into the versions array.
+func (s storage) UpsertHandsetModel(ctx context.Context, handset models.Handset) error {
+    // Fetch the existing document to determine if currentProperties has changed
+    var existing models.Handset
+    err := s.handsetsCollection.FindOne(ctx, bson.M{"billID": handset.BillID}).Decode(&existing)
+    if err != nil && !errors.Is(err, mongo.ErrNoDocuments) {
+        return fmt.Errorf("could not fetch existing handset: %w", err)
     }
 
-    _, err := s.handsetsCollection.
-        UpdateOne(ctx, bson.M{"id": handset.ID}, set, options.Update().SetUpsert(true))
+    update := bson.M{}
+
+    if err == nil {
+        // Document exists – push old currentProperties into versions if version changed
+        if existing.CurrentProperties.Version != "" && existing.CurrentProperties.Version != handset.CurrentProperties.Version {
+            update["$push"] = bson.M{"versions": existing.CurrentProperties}
+        }
+    }
+
+    // Ensure newly inserted handsets have a stable UUID id.
+    update["$setOnInsert"] = bson.M{
+        "id": uuid.New(),
+    }
+
+    update["$set"] = bson.M{
+        "billID":            handset.BillID,
+        "active":            handset.Active,
+        "currentProperties": handset.CurrentProperties,
+    }
+
+    _, err = s.handsetsCollection.
+        UpdateOne(ctx, bson.M{"billID": handset.BillID}, update, options.Update().SetUpsert(true))
     if err != nil {
         return fmt.Errorf("could not upsert handset: %w", err)
     }
@@ -116,8 +152,11 @@ func (s storage) UpsertHandset(ctx context.Context, handset handsetdb.Handset) e
     return nil
 }

+func (s storage) UpdateContractEligibilityApproved(ctx context.Context, requestID string, outcome models.EligibilityOutcome) error {
+    setFields := bson.M{
+        "status":    models.ContractStatusEligibilityApproved,
+        "updatedAt": time.Now(),
+    }
+    if outcome.Decision != "" {
+        setFields["decision"] = outcome.Decision
+    }
+    if outcome.AgreementID != "" {
+        setFields["agreementId"] = outcome.AgreementID
+    }
+    if outcome.DocusignEnvelopeID != "" {
+        setFields["docusignEnvelopeId"] = outcome.DocusignEnvelopeID
+    }
+    if outcome.SignedAt != nil {
+        setFields["signedAt"] = outcome.SignedAt
+    }
+    if outcome.CompletedAt != nil {
+        setFields["completedAt"] = outcome.CompletedAt
+    }
+
+    filter := bson.M{
+        "requestId": requestID,
+        "status":    models.ContractStatusPendingEligibility,
+    }
+    result, err := s.contractsCollection.UpdateOne(ctx, filter, bson.M{"$set": setFields})
+    if err != nil {
+        return fmt.Errorf("could not update contract eligibility: %w", err)
+    }
+    if result.MatchedCount == 0 {
+        return terrors.ErrConflict
+    }
+    return nil
+}
+
+func (s storage) UpdateContractEligibilityFailed(ctx context.Context, requestID string, outcome models.EligibilityFailureOutcome) error {
+    setFields := bson.M{
+        "status":    models.ContractStatusDeclined,
+        "updatedAt": time.Now(),
+    }
+    if outcome.FailureReason != "" {
+        setFields["failureReason"] = outcome.FailureReason
+    }
+    if outcome.FailureStage != "" {
+        setFields["failureStage"] = outcome.FailureStage
+    }
+    if outcome.FailureMessage != "" {
+        setFields["failureMessage"] = outcome.FailureMessage
+    }
+    if outcome.FailedAt != nil {
+        setFields["failedAt"] = outcome.FailedAt
+    }
+
+    filter := bson.M{
+        "requestId": requestID,
+        "status":    models.ContractStatusPendingEligibility,
+    }
+    result, err := s.contractsCollection.UpdateOne(ctx, filter, bson.M{"$set": setFields})
+    if err != nil {
+        return fmt.Errorf("could not update contract eligibility failure: %w", err)
+    }
+    if result.MatchedCount == 0 {
+        return terrors.ErrConflict
+    }
+    return nil
+}
